Can you believe that in Jacksonville FL, the LARGEST city in the continental US (land wise), we don't have a Mongolian BBQ place!? Ah! We did eat at GK off Coffee Rd. once and that tore me up for a day or so - so we don't go back there.

I choose beef and load up with carrots, water chestnuts, bean sprouts, and cabbage. They add the oils and I like mine spicy (Siracha!). They cook your dish right in front of you on the Mongolian Grill and it's done! It's flavorful and I am so happy to come and eat here! Nice place to grab a good boba creation. They have a wide variety to choose from or create your own. Our favorite is the 'Sunset Dream' a butterfly milk tea infused with strawberries and a colorful burst of flavors. Also added touch is the boba. Once mixed up it will turn a nice lavender color.  In door seating & parking lot seating is closed. Take out and delivery service are only options available at this time. Hand sanitizer stations located throughout the store. Prices are reasonable and fall into line with most of the other boba lounges. Those bacon waffle fries are pretty tasty. Called 'bacon & cream'. These are waffle fries with bacon , green bell peppers, sour cream and sprinkled with chives. Oh yeah. Can't forget one of those 'sunset dream' boba.</text>

Happened to be in West Covina for a dental appointment l. I was thirsty and in the mode for boba tea. So I looked up Yelp and found a boba tea place nearby with over 800 reviews. I thought it must  be good.

< name>
Lawrence Thai<//name>
<Rating>4</Rating>< Review>
I've come here a few times and every single time has been a good experience.

BYOB sits in the same plaza as the HK supermarket, and although BYOB can be a bit hard to find, just look out for the market than you will be in the right place. Parking here can sometimes be hard to find during peak hours as all the restaurants as well as how busy the market can get will fill up the parking lot at times.

Now lets get to the review. The inside of the store is nicely decorate, with a few tables in the front and high tables towards the back. They had also recently added some claw machines inside which is a nice plus. There are also restrooms here. The service here is almost always great, except a few times where I felt like it could have been better.

The drinks here are great. I've only tried a handful of drinks though, but they were all excellent. There was one times though where I ordered a Boba Milk Tea and it was way too sweet. I haven't tried any of the food here yet so that is an addition to this review in the future.

Overall, I always find my way back here despite a few instances where I felt like it could've been better. Because of that, I felt like giving it 4 stars would be a more honest rating.< /Review>

<user>111786517743281339317<//user>< username>

<Time>1440144338810<//Time><Rating>3<//Rating><Text>I've tried BYOB twice now, and both time I've left feeling underwhelmed. BYOB is different from other boba shops in that you are able to customize your own drinks and toppings from a variety of assortments if you don't want to order a drink off of their menu.

Upon first glance, it is quite overwhelming as there are teas, toppings, flavors, drizzles you can customize into your drink. The workers are very quick to give you a hand and take you through the process, especially if it's your first time at BYOB. Basically pick a size, if you want it blended or shaken, with tea, milk, flavor ... any drizzles, and then fill it up with toppings!

The first time I tried BYOB, I ordered an almond milk tea and added boba, almond pudding, and egg pudding to my drink. I really like boba and pudding, and I can definitely drink a large amount of toppings, so I asked the worker to pack my cup! There wasn't a set price on customizing my drink, and since I had ordered almond milk tea, I was able to get the drink priced as something off of their milk tea menu. The drink was pretty good, but nowhere near quality tea. I feel like the almond tea tasted pre-made, sweet with artificial almond flavor. The boba and pudding were good, but nothing too memorable.

My friends ordered random drinks and they all thought their drinks were pretty good. I tried the Orange Blossom, almond Hokkaido milk tea ... they were okay, but a little too artificial tasting. Overall, it was a very interesting experience being able to order whatever we wanted. My friend even told the worker she liked grapefruit, and he was able to whip up something that she really liked.

The second time I returned, I tried their Lost at Sea creation, a sea salt green tea, with boba. I had wanted to get the almond milk tea again, but I guess the prices have changed since I've been, and making my own drink cost way more than trying a creation of BYOB's. Lost at Sea wasn't a bad drink, but it definitely wasn't a good one that I'd get again. It tasted sweet, but didn't have any tea flavor. Boba was nice and chewy, but the drink itself was really bad.

BYOB is also known for remaking drinks if you're unsatisfied with the taste. (A good thing, but what happens to all those drinks people don't like!) Unfortunately I was in a rush and couldn't fix my drink. Overall, it's a good concept if you're into building your own drinks and whatnot, but I prefer drinking boba that has good quality tea alongside of it.<//Text><pictures>None<//pictures><response>None< /response><GmapID>0x80c2d62d9564ad25:0xfb5549049cbaa109< /GmapID></record></dataset><record>

<UserId.>110973711623683010244<//UserId.><Name>Lindsey Dillon</Name><date>1485551663492</date><rating>3< /rating>< text>
The diner is cutesy in that overly flowery grandma kinda way and it smells inviting. I originally came to try out the chocolate biscuits and gravy.

I ordered the Mediterranean Omelet with hash browns and the chocolate biscuits and gravy. My fiance had the waffle combo. The service was good, we were seated quickly, our waitress was friendly and our drinks were refilled regularly, but I found the food lacking.

My omelet had an overly large amount of feta in it and my hash browns were cooked together in a large clump. Pretty much like fried mashed potatoes, nothing like regular hash browns.

I was very disappointed in the chocolate biscuits and gravy. The biscuits were pretty standard breakfast biscuits, nothing to write home about, but the chocolate tasted disgusting. It was overly sweet and tasted like instant pudding, which I hate. My fiance's bacon was also pretty much jerky, way too chewy.</text>
